metrics:\\n  - Spearman rank correlation instead of Pearson\\n  - Classify into \\\"easy\\\" vs \\\"hard\\\" (binary) instead of 3-class\\n  - Use Mann-Whitney U test for significance\\n- Skip real datasets fail to load, generate synthetic validation data:\\n  - Create texts with controlled semantic coherence (e.g., coherent paragraph vs. randomly shuffled sentences)\\n  - Verify that SCD captures the coherence difference\\n  - This at least validates that the metric is sensitive to semantic flow\",\n  \"testing_plan\": \"Testing strategy for the experiment implementation:\\n\\n**Phase1: Unit Tests (Pre-Experiment)**\\n1. Test sentence tokenization:\\n   ```python\\n   text = \\\"This is sentence one. This is sentence two! Is this sentence three?\\\"\\n   sentences = sentence_tokenize(text)\\n   assert len(sentences) == 3\\n   ```\\n\\n2. Test SCD computation on known inputs:\\n   ```python\\n   # Coherent text (should have low SCD)\\n   coherent = \\\"The cat sat on the mat. The mat was comfortable. The cat enjoyed sitting.\\\"\\n   scd_coherent = compute_scd(coherent, method=\\\"cosine\\\")\\n   \\n   # Incoherent text (should have high SCD)\\n   incoherent = \\\"The cat sat on the mat. Quantum mechanics describes particle behavior. Bananas are yellow fruits.\\\"\\n   scd_incoherent = compute_scd(incoherent, method=\\\"cosine\\\")\\n   \\n   assert scd_incoherent > scd_coherent, \\\"SCD should be higher for incoherent text\\\"\\n   ```\\n\\n3. Test readability formulas on known examples:\\n   ```python\\n   simple_text = \\\"The cat sat. The dog ran. Kids played.\\\"\\n   complex_text = \\\"The juxtaposition of lexicographical elements necessitates methodological recalibration.\\\"\\n   \\n   simple_fk = textstat.flesch_kincaid_grade(simple_text)\\n   complex_fk = textstat.flesch_kincaid_grade(complex_text)\\n   \\n   assert simple_fk < complex_fk, \\\"Simple text should have lower grade level\\\"\\n   ```\\n\\n**Phase 2: Integration Tests (Small Scale)**\\n1. Run on mini dataset (3 examples per dataset):\\n   ```bash\\n   uv run python experiment_scd_readability.py --mini  # Use mini_data_out.json\\n   ```\\n   - Verify all methods compute without errors\\n   - Check output JSON structure\\n   - Verify plots are generated\\n\\n2. =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 1: Load and Validate Data\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 1: Loading datasets...\\\")\\n    \\n    data_path = Path(\\\"../iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1/full_data_out.json\\\")\\n    with open(data_path, 'r') as f:\\n        data = json.load(f)\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 2: Initialize Models\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 2: Initializing SBERT model...\\\")\\n    \\n    # Load SBERT model (all-MiniLM-L6-v2 = 384 dimensions, fast inference)\\n    sbert_model = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\\n    logger.info(f\\\"SBERT model loaded: {sbert_model.get_sentence_embedding_dimension()}D embeddings\\\")\\n    \\n    # Initialize textstat (no setup needed, but set language)\\n    textstat.set_lang('en')\\n    logger.info(\\\"textstat initialized\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 3: Implement SCD Metric\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 3: Implementing SCD computation...\\\")\\n    \\n    def sentence_tokenize(text: str) -> List[str]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Simple sentence tokenization.\\n        Splits on [.!?] followed by whitespace or end-of-string.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        # Split on sentence endings\\n        sentences = re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\\\\s+', text.strip())\\n        # Filter empty sentences\\n        sentences = [s.strip() for s in sentences if s.strip()]\\n        return sentences\\n    \\n    def compute_scd(text: str, method: str = \\\"cosine\\\") -> float:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute Semantic Coherence Distance for a text.\\n        \\n        Args:\\n            text: Input text\\n            method: \\\"cosine\\\" or \\\"euclidean\\\"\\n        \\n        Returns:\\n            SCD score (normalized by sentence count)\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        sentences = sentence_tokenize(text)\\n        \\n        if len(sentences) < 2:\\n            return 0.0  # Single sentence = perfect coherence\\n        \\n        # Encode sentences\\n        embeddings = sbert_model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n        \\n        # Compute pairwise distances between consecutive sentences\\n        distances = []\\n        for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n            if method == \\\"cosine\\\":\\n                # Cosine distance = 1 - cosine_similarity\\n                cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n                dist = 1 - cos_sim\\n            elif method == \\\"euclidean\\\":\\n                # Squared Euclidean distance\\n                diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n                dist = np.sum(diff**2)\\n            else:\\n                raise ValueError(f\\\"Unknown method: {method}\\\")\\n            distances.append(dist)\\n        \\n        # Average distance (normalize by sentence count)\\n        scd = np.mean(distances)\\n        return float(scd)\\n    \\n    def compute_scd_variants(text: str) -> Dict[str, float]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute multiple SCD variants for ablation.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        sentences = sentence_tokenize(text)\\n        if len(sentences) < 2:\\n            return {\\n                \\\"scd_cosine\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_euclidean\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_cosine_norm\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_euclidean_norm\\\": 0.0,\\n            }\\n        \\n        embeddings = sbert_model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n        \\n        # Cosine distances\\n        cos_dists = []\\n        eucl_dists = []\\n        for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n            # Cosine\\n            cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n            cos_dists.append(1 - cos_sim)\\n            # Euclidean\\n            diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n            eucl_dists.append(np.sum(diff**2))\\n        \\n        return {\\n            \\\"scd_cosine\\\": np.mean(cos_dists),\\n            \\\"scd_euclidean\\\": np.mean(eucl_dists),\\n            \\\"scd_cosine_norm\\\": np.mean(cos_dists) / len(sentences),  # Normalize by sent count\\n            \\\"scd_euclidean_norm\\\": np.mean(eucl_dists) / len(sentences),\\n        }\\n    \\n    logger.info(\\\"SCD functions defined\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 4: Implement Baseline Readability Formulas\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 4: Implementing baseline readability formulas...\\\")\\n    \\n    def compute_readability_scores(text: str) -> Dict[str, float]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute all baseline readability formulas using textstat.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        scores = {}\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_kincaid\\\"] = textstat.flesch_kincaid_grade(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_kincaid\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"smog\\\"] = textstat.smog_index(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"smog\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"coleman_liau\\\"] = textstat.coleman_liau_index(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"coleman_liau\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"dale_chall\\\"] = textstat.dale_chall_readability_score(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"dale_chall\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"ari\\\"] = textstat.automated_readability_index(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"ari\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_reading_ease\\\"] = textstat.flesch_reading_ease(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_reading_ease\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        return scores\\n    \\n    logger.info(\\\"Baseline formulas defined\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 5: Compute Metrics for All Datasets\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 5: Computing metrics for all examples...\\\")\\n    \\n    results = {\\n        \\\"metadata\\\": {\\n            \\\"description\\\": \\\"SCD vs Baseline Readability Formulas Experiment\\\",\\n            \\\"datasets\\\": list(datasets.keys()),\\n            \\\"methods\\\": [\\\"scd_cosine\\\", \\\"scd_euclidean\\\", \\\"flesch_kincaid\\\", \\\"smog\\\", \\\"coleman_liau\\\", \\\"dale_chall\\\", \\\"ari\\\"]\\n        },\\n        \\\"results_by_dataset\\\": {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    for dataset_name, examples in datasets.items():\\n        logger.info(f\\\"Processing {dataset_name} ({len(examples)} examples)...\\\")\\n        \\n        dataset_results = []\\n        \\n        for i, example in enumerate(examples):\\n            if i % 100 == 0:\\n                logger.info(f\\\"  Processing example {i}/{len(examples)}...\\\")\\n            \\n            text = example[\\\"input\\\"]\\n            \\n            # Compute SCD variants\\n            scd_scores = compute_scd_variants(text)\\n            \\n            # Compute baseline readability scores\\n            readability_scores = compute_readability_scores(text)\\n            \\n            # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 6: Statistical Evaluation\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 6: Computing correlations and classification metrics...\\\")\\n    \\n    evaluation_results = {\\n        \\\"clear_corpus\\\": {},\\n        \\\"onestop_english\\\": {},\\n        \\\"wikilarge\\\": {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    # CLEAR Corpus: Correlation with Human Judgments\\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    logger.info(\\\"Evaluating CLEAR Corpus (correlation with human judgments)...\\\")\\n    \\n    clear_data = results[\\\"results_by_dataset\\\"][\\\"clear_corpus\\\"]\\n    \\n    # Extract valid examples (with human readability scores)\\n    valid_clear = [d for d in clear_data if d[\\\"human_readability\\\"] is not None]\\n    logger.info(f\\\"  Valid examples for CLEAR: {len(valid_clear)}/{len(clear_data)}\\\")\\n    \\n    if len(valid_clear) > 10:\\n        # Prepare data for correlation\\n        y_human = np.array([d[\\\"human_readability\\\"] for d in valid_clear])\\n        \\n        correlations = {}\\n        \\n        # Methods to evaluate\\n        methods = [\\\"scd_cosine\\\", \\\"scd_euclidean\\\", \\\"flesch_kincaid\\\", \\\"smog\\\", \\\"coleman_liau\\\", \\\"dale_chall\\\", \\\"ari\\\", \\\"flesch_reading_ease\\\"]\\n        \\n        for method in methods:\\n            # Extract scores for this method\\n            x_scores = np.array([d[\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan) for d in valid_clear])\\n            \\n            # Remove NaN values\\n            valid_idx = ~np.isnan(x_scores)\\n            x_valid = x_scores[valid_idx]\\n            y_valid = y_human[valid_idx]\\n            \\n            if len(x_valid) < 10:\\n                logger.warning(f\\\"  Insufficient valid data for {method}\\\")\\n                correlations[method] = {\\\"pearson_r\\\": np.nan, \\\"p_value\\\": np.nan, \\\"n\\\": 0}\\n                continue\\n            \\n            # Compute Pearson correlation\\n            r, p = pearsonr(x_valid, y_valid)\\n            \\n            # Bootstrap 95% CI for correlation\\n            def corr_func(data):\\n                return np.corrcoef(data[0], data[1])[0, 1]\\n            \\n            boot_result = bootstrap(\\n                data=(x_valid, y_valid),\\n                statistic=corr_func,\\n                confidence_level=0.95,\\n                n_resamples=1000,\\n                method='percentile'\\n            )\\n            \\n            correlations[method] = {\\n                \\\"pearson_r\\\": float(r),\\n                \\\"p_value\\\": float(p),\\n                \\\"ci_95_lower\\\": float(boot_result.confidence_interval.low),\\n                \\\"ci_95_upper\\\": float(boot_result.confidence_interval.high),\\n                \\\"n\\\": int(len(x_valid))\\n            }\\n            \\n            logger.info(f\\\"  {method}: r={r:.3f} (95% CI [{boot_result.confidence_interval.low:.3f}, {boot_result.confidence_interval.high:.3f}]), p={p:.4f}, n={len(x_valid)}\\\")\\n        \\n        evaluation_results[\\\"clear_corpus\\\"][\\\"correlations\\\"] = correlations\\n    \\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    # OneStopEnglish: Classification (3 difficulty levels)\\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    logger.info(\\\"Evaluating OneStopEnglish (3-class classification)...\\\")\\n    \\n    ose_data = results[\\\"results_by_dataset\\\"][\\\"onestop_english\\\"]\\n    \\n    # Prepare data\\n        y_true = np.array([int(d[\\\"difficulty_level\\\"]) for d in valid_ose])  # 1, 2, or 3\\n        \\n        classification_results = {}\\n        \\n        for method in methods:\\n            # Extract scores\\n            x_scores = np.array([d[\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan) for d in valid_ose])\\n            \\n            # Remove NaN\\n            valid_idx = ~np.isnan(x_scores)\\n            x_valid = x_scores[valid_idx]\\n            y_valid = y_true[valid_idx]\\n            \\n            if len(x_valid) < 10:\\n                classification_results[method] = {\\\"accuracy\\\": np.nan, \\\"f1_macro\\\": np.nan, \\\"n\\\": 0}\\n                continue\\n            \\n            # Simple threshold-based classification\\n            # For readability scores: lower = easier (typically)\\n            # For SCD: higher = less coherent = harder (hypothesis)\\n            \\n            # Use median split for 3-class (simple baseline)\\n            if method.startswith(\\\"scd\\\"):\\n                # Higher SCD = harder, so invert for classification\\n                x_for_classify = -x_valid\\n            else:\\n                x_for_classify = x_valid\\n            \\n            # Simple classification: split into 3 quantiles\\n            from sklearn.tree import DecisionTreeClassifier\\n            from sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score\\n            \\n            clf = DecisionTreeClassifier(max_depth=3, random_state=42)\\n            cv_scores = cross_val_score(clf, x_for_classify.reshape(-1, 1), y_valid, cv=5, scoring='accuracy')\\n            cv_f1 = cross_val_score(clf, x_for_classify.reshape(-1, 1), y_valid, cv=5, scoring='f1_macro')\\n            \\n            classification_results[method] = {\\n                \\\"accuracy_mean\\\": float(np.mean(cv_scores)),\\n                \\\"accuracy_std\\\": float(np.std(cv_scores)),\\n                \\\"f1_macro_mean\\\": float(np.mean(cv_f1)),\\n                \\\"f1_macro_std\\\": float(np.std(cv_f1)),\\n                \\\"n\\\": int(len(x_valid))\\n            }\\n            \\n            logger.info(f\\\"  {method}: accuracy={np.mean(cv_scores):.3f} (+/- {np.std(cv_scores):.3f}), f1={np.mean(cv_f1):.3f}, n={len(x_valid)}\\\")\\n        \\n        evaluation_results[\\\"onestop_english\\\"][\\\"classification\\\"] = classification_results\\n    \\n    # Evaluate ranking (simple should have lower readability score than normal)\\n    ranking_results = {}\\n    \\n    for method in methods:\\n        correct = 0\\n        total = 0\\n        \\n        for pair_key, pair_data in pairs.items():\\n            if \\\"simple\\\" not in pair_data or \\\"normal\\\" not in pair_data:\\n                continue\\n            \\n            simple_score = pair_data[\\\"simple\\\"][\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan)\\n            normal_score = pair_data[\\\"normal\\\"][\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan)\\n            \\n            if np.isnan(simple_score) or np.isnan(normal_score):\\n                continue\\n            \\n            # For traditional formulas: simple < normal (lower grade level)\\n            # For SCD: hypothesis is that simple has lower SCD (more coherent)\\n            if method.startswith(\\\"scd\\\"):\\n                # Lower SCD = more coherent = simpler\\n                if simple_score < normal_score:\\n                    correct += 1\\n            else:\\n                # Lower grade level = simpler\\n                if simple_score < normal_score:\\n                    correct += 1\\n            \\n            total += 1\\n        \\n        if total > 0:\\n            accuracy = correct / total\\n        else:\\n            accuracy = np.nan\\n        \\n        ranking_results[method] = {\\n            \\\"ranking_accuracy\\\": float(accuracy),\\n            \\\"n_pairs\\\": int(total)\\n        }\\n        \\n        logger.info(f\\\"  {method}: ranking accuracy={accuracy:.3f} ({correct}/{total})\\\")\\n    \\n    evaluation_results[\\\"wikilarge\\\"][\\\"ranking\\\"] = ranking_results\\n    \\n    # \\\"textstat_per_doc\\\": float(textstat_time),\\n        \\\"notes\\\": \\\"Average over 10 runs on sample document\\\"\\n    }\\n    \\n    logger.info(f\\\"  SBERT encoding: {sbert_time*1000:.1f}ms Single sentence = perfect coherence\\n        \\n        # Encode sentences\\n        embeddings = sbert_model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n        \\n        # Compute pairwise distances between consecutive sentences\\n        distances = []\\n        for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n            if method == \\\"cosine\\\":\\n                # Cosine distance = 1 - cosine_similarity\\n                cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n                dist = 1 - cos_sim\\n            elif method == \\\"euclidean\\\":\\n                # Squared Euclidean distance\\n                diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n                dist = np.sum(diff**2)\\n            else:\\n                raise ValueError(f\\\"Unknown method: {method}\\\")\\n            distances.append(dist)\\n        \\n        # Average distance (normalize by sentence count)\\n        scd = np.mean(distances)\\n        return float(scd)\\n    \\n    def compute_scd_variants(text: str) -> Dict[str, float]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute multiple SCD variants for ablation.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        sentences = sentence_tokenize(text)\\n        if len(sentences) < 2:\\n            return {\\n                \\\"scd_cosine\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_euclidean\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_cosine_norm\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_euclidean_norm\\\": 0.0,\\n            }\\n        \\n        embeddings = sbert_model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n        \\n        # Cosine distances\\n        cos_dists = []\\n        eucl_dists = []\\n        for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n            # Cosine\\n            cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n            cos_dists.append(1 - cos_sim)\\n            # Euclidean\\n            diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n            eucl_dists.append(np.sum(diff**2))\\n        \\n        return {\\n            \\\"scd_cosine\\\": np.mean(cos_dists),\\n            \\\"scd_euclidean\\\": np.mean(eucl_dists),\\n            \\\"scd_cosine_norm\\\": np.mean(cos_dists) / len(sentences),  # Normalize by sent count\\n            \\\"scd_euclidean_norm\\\": np.mean(eucl_dists) / len(sentences),\\n        }\\n    \\n    logger.info(\\\"SCD functions defined\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # {"content": [{"cache_prompt": false, "type": "text", "text": "NOTE: We only show up to 8 since there're only 8 lines in this file.\nHere's the result of running `cat -n` on /ai-inventor/aii_data/runs/run_6uOr5GlpaMfR/3_invention_loop/iter_2/gen_plan/gen_plan_experiment_1/.sdk_openhands_agent_struct_out.json:\n     1\t{\n     2\t  \"title\": \"Test Semantic Coherence Distance for Readability\",\n     3\t  \"summary\": \"Evaluate whether semantic coherence distance (SCD) using SBERT embeddings correlates with human readability judgments and can classify text difficulty levels, comparing against traditional readability formulas on CLEAR and OneStopEnglish datasets.\",\n     4\t  \"runpod_compute_profile\": \"cpu_heavy\",\n     5\t  \"implementation_pseudocode\": \"MAIN EXPERIMENT SCRIPT (experiment_scd_readability.py):\\n\\n```python\\n#!/usr/bin/env python3\\n\\\"\\\"\\\"Experiment: Evaluate Semantic Coherence Distance for Readability Assessment\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n\\nimport json\\nimport numpy as np\\nfrom pathlib import Path\\nfrom loguru import logger\\nimport sys\\nimport time\\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Tuple, Any\\nimport re\\n\\n# ML/NLP libraries\\nfrom sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer\\nimport textstat\\nfrom sklearn.metrics import pearsonr, classification_report, accuracy_score, f1_score\\nfrom scipy.stats import bootstrap\\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\\n\\nlogger.remove()\\nlogger.add(sys.stdout, level=\\\"INFO\\\", format=\\\"{time:HH:mm:ss}|{level:<7}|{message}\\\")\\nlogger.add(\\\"logs/run.log\\\", rotation=\\\"50 MB\\\", level=\\\"DEBUG\\\")\\n\\n@logger.catch(reraise=True)\\ndef main():\\n    \\\"\\\"\\\"Main experiment logic.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 1: Load and Validate Data\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 1: Loading datasets...\\\")\\n    \\n    data_path = Path(\\\"../iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1/full_data_out.json\\\")\\n    with open(data_path, 'r') as f:\\n        data = json.load(f)\\n    \\n    # Extract datasets\\n    datasets = {d[\\\"dataset\\\"]: d[\\\"examples\\\"] for d in data[\\\"datasets\\\"]}\\n    \\n    logger.info(f\\\"Loaded datasets: {list(datasets.keys())}\\\")\\n    for name, examples in datasets.items():\\n        logger.info(f\\\"  {name}: {len(examples)} examples\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 2: Initialize Models\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 2: Initializing SBERT model...\\\")\\n    \\n    # Load SBERT model (all-MiniLM-L6-v2 = 384 dimensions, fast inference)\\n    sbert_model = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\\n    logger.info(f\\\"SBERT model loaded: {sbert_model.get_sentence_embedding_dimension()}D embeddings\\\")\\n    \\n    # Initialize textstat (no setup needed, but set language)\\n    textstat.set_lang('en')\\n    logger.info(\\\"textstat initialized\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 3: Implement SCD Metric\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 3: Implementing SCD computation...\\\")\\n    \\n    def sentence_tokenize(text: str) -> List[str]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Simple sentence tokenization.\\n        Splits on [.!?] followed by whitespace or end-of-string.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        # Split on sentence endings\\n        sentences = re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\\\\s+', text.strip())\\n        # Filter empty sentences\\n        sentences = [s.strip() for s in sentences if s.strip()]\\n        return sentences\\n    \\n    def compute_scd(text: str, method: str = \\\"cosine\\\") -> float:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute Semantic Coherence Distance for a text.\\n        \\n        Args:\\n            text: Input text\\n            method: \\\"cosine\\\" or \\\"euclidean\\\"\\n        \\n        Returns:\\n            SCD score (normalized by sentence count)\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        sentences = sentence_tokenize(text)\\n        \\n        if len(sentences) < 2:\\n            return 0.0  # Single sentence = perfect coherence\\n        \\n        # Encode sentences\\n        embeddings = sbert_model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n        \\n        # Compute pairwise distances between consecutive sentences\\n        distances = []\\n        for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n            if method == \\\"cosine\\\":\\n                # Cosine distance = 1 - cosine_similarity\\n                cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n                dist = 1 - cos_sim\\n            elif method == \\\"euclidean\\\":\\n                # Squared Euclidean distance\\n                diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n                dist = np.sum(diff**2)\\n            else:\\n                raise ValueError(f\\\"Unknown method: {method}\\\")\\n            distances.append(dist)\\n        \\n        # Average distance (normalize by sentence count)\\n        scd = np.mean(distances)\\n        return float(scd)\\n    \\n    def compute_scd_variants(text: str) -> Dict[str, float]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute multiple SCD variants for ablation.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        sentences = sentence_tokenize(text)\\n        if len(sentences) < 2:\\n            return {\\n                \\\"scd_cosine\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_euclidean\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_cosine_norm\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_euclidean_norm\\\": 0.0,\\n            }\\n        \\n        embeddings = sbert_model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n        \\n        # Cosine distances\\n        cos_dists = []\\n        eucl_dists = []\\n        for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n            # Cosine\\n            cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n            cos_dists.append(1 - cos_sim)\\n            # Euclidean\\n            diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n            eucl_dists.append(np.sum(diff**2))\\n        \\n        return {\\n            \\\"scd_cosine\\\": np.mean(cos_dists),\\n            \\\"scd_euclidean\\\": np.mean(eucl_dists),\\n            \\\"scd_cosine_norm\\\": np.mean(cos_dists) / len(sentences),  # Normalize by sent count\\n            \\\"scd_euclidean_norm\\\": np.mean(eucl_dists) / len(sentences),\\n        }\\n    \\n    logger.info(\\\"SCD functions defined\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # Sentence tokenization:\\n   ```python\\n   import re\\n   sentences = re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\\\\s+', text.strip())\\n   sentences = [s.strip() for s in sentences if s.strip()]\\n   ```\\n   - Handles '.', '!', '?' as sentence terminators\\n   - Filters empty strings\\n\\n2. SBERT encoding:\\n   ```python\\n   embeddings = model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n   ```\\n   - Returns numpy array of shape (n_sentences, 384)\\n   - Batch processing is automatic\\n\\n3. Compute distances between consecutive sentences:\\n   ```python\\n   cos_dists = []\\n   eucl_dists = []\\n   for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n       # Cosine distance = 1 - cosine_similarity\\n       cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n       cos_dists.append(1 - cos_sim)\\n       \\n       # Squared Euclidean distance\\n       diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n       eucl_dists.append(np.sum(diff**2))\\n   ```\\n\\n4. =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 1: Load and Validate Data\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 1: Loading datasets...\\\")\\n    \\n    data_path = Path(\\\"../iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1/full_data_out.json\\\")\\n    with open(data_path, 'r') as f:\\n        data = json.load(f)\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 2: Initialize Models\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 2: Initializing SBERT model...\\\")\\n    \\n    # Load SBERT model (all-MiniLM-L6-v2 = 384 dimensions, fast inference)\\n    sbert_model = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\\n    logger.info(f\\\"SBERT model loaded: {sbert_model.get_sentence_embedding_dimension()}D embeddings\\\")\\n    \\n    # Initialize textstat (no setup needed, but set language)\\n    textstat.set_lang('en')\\n    logger.info(\\\"textstat initialized\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 3: Implement SCD Metric\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 3: Implementing SCD computation...\\\")\\n    \\n    def sentence_tokenize(text: str) -> List[str]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Simple sentence tokenization.\\n        Splits on [.!?] followed by whitespace or end-of-string.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        # Split on sentence endings\\n        sentences = re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\\\\s+', text.strip())\\n        # Filter empty sentences\\n        sentences = [s.strip() for s in sentences if s.strip()]\\n        return sentences\\n    \\n    def compute_scd(text: str, method: str = \\\"cosine\\\") -> float:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute Semantic Coherence Distance for a text.\\n        \\n        Args:\\n            text: Input text\\n            method: \\\"cosine\\\" or \\\"euclidean\\\"\\n        \\n        Returns:\\n            SCD score (normalized by sentence count)\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        sentences = sentence_tokenize(text)\\n        \\n        if len(sentences) < 2:\\n            return 0.0  # Single sentence = perfect coherence\\n        \\n        # Encode sentences\\n        embeddings = sbert_model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n        \\n        # Compute pairwise distances between consecutive sentences\\n        distances = []\\n        for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n            if method == \\\"cosine\\\":\\n                # Cosine distance = 1 - cosine_similarity\\n                cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n                dist = 1 - cos_sim\\n            elif method == \\\"euclidean\\\":\\n                # Squared Euclidean distance\\n                diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n                dist = np.sum(diff**2)\\n            else:\\n                raise ValueError(f\\\"Unknown method: {method}\\\")\\n            distances.append(dist)\\n        \\n        # Average distance (normalize by sentence count)\\n        scd = np.mean(distances)\\n        return float(scd)\\n    \\n    def compute_scd_variants(text: str) -> Dict[str, float]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute multiple SCD variants for ablation.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        sentences = sentence_tokenize(text)\\n        if len(sentences) < 2:\\n            return {\\n                \\\"scd_cosine\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_euclidean\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_cosine_norm\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_euclidean_norm\\\": 0.0,\\n            }\\n        \\n        embeddings = sbert_model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n        \\n        # Cosine distances\\n        cos_dists = []\\n        eucl_dists = []\\n        for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n            # Cosine\\n            cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n            cos_dists.append(1 - cos_sim)\\n            # Euclidean\\n            diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n            eucl_dists.append(np.sum(diff**2))\\n        \\n        return {\\n            \\\"scd_cosine\\\": np.mean(cos_dists),\\n            \\\"scd_euclidean\\\": np.mean(eucl_dists),\\n            \\\"scd_cosine_norm\\\": np.mean(cos_dists) / len(sentences),  # Normalize by sent count\\n            \\\"scd_euclidean_norm\\\": np.mean(eucl_dists) / len(sentences),\\n        }\\n    \\n    logger.info(\\\"SCD functions defined\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 4: Implement Baseline Readability Formulas\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 4: Implementing baseline readability formulas...\\\")\\n    \\n    def compute_readability_scores(text: str) -> Dict[str, float]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute all baseline readability formulas using textstat.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        scores = {}\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_kincaid\\\"] = textstat.flesch_kincaid_grade(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_kincaid\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"smog\\\"] = textstat.smog_index(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"smog\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"coleman_liau\\\"] = textstat.coleman_liau_index(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"coleman_liau\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"dale_chall\\\"] = textstat.dale_chall_readability_score(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"dale_chall\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"ari\\\"] = textstat.automated_readability_index(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"ari\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_reading_ease\\\"] = textstat.flesch_reading_ease(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_reading_ease\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        return scores\\n    \\n    logger.info(\\\"Baseline formulas defined\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 5: Compute Metrics for All Datasets\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 5: Computing metrics for all examples...\\\")\\n    \\n    results = {\\n        \\\"metadata\\\": {\\n            \\\"description\\\": \\\"SCD vs Baseline Readability Formulas Experiment\\\",\\n            \\\"datasets\\\": list(datasets.keys()),\\n            \\\"methods\\\": [\\\"scd_cosine\\\", \\\"scd_euclidean\\\", \\\"flesch_kincaid\\\", \\\"smog\\\", \\\"coleman_liau\\\", \\\"dale_chall\\\", \\\"ari\\\"]\\n        },\\n        \\\"results_by_dataset\\\": {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    for dataset_name, examples in datasets.items():\\n        logger.info(f\\\"Processing {dataset_name} ({len(examples)} examples)...\\\")\\n        \\n        dataset_results = []\\n        \\n        for i, example in enumerate(examples):\\n            if i % 100 == 0:\\n                logger.info(f\\\"  Processing example {i}/{len(examples)}...\\\")\\n            \\n            text = example[\\\"input\\\"]\\n            \\n            # Compute SCD variants\\n            scd_scores = compute_scd_variants(text)\\n            \\n            # Compute baseline readability scores\\n            readability_scores = compute_readability_scores(text)\\n            \\n            # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    # CLEAR Corpus: Correlation with Human Judgments\\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    logger.info(\\\"Evaluating CLEAR Corpus (correlation with human judgments)...\\\")\\n    \\n    clear_data = results[\\\"results_by_dataset\\\"][\\\"clear_corpus\\\"]\\n    \\n    # Extract valid examples (with human readability scores)\\n    valid_clear = [d for d in clear_data if d[\\\"human_readability\\\"] is not None]\\n    logger.info(f\\\"  Valid examples for CLEAR: {len(valid_clear)}/{len(clear_data)}\\\")\\n    \\n    if len(valid_clear) > 10:\\n        # Prepare data for correlation\\n        y_human = np.array([d[\\\"human_readability\\\"] for d in valid_clear])\\n        \\n        correlations = {}\\n        \\n        # Methods to evaluate\\n        methods = [\\\"scd_cosine\\\", \\\"scd_euclidean\\\", \\\"flesch_kincaid\\\", \\\"smog\\\", \\\"coleman_liau\\\", \\\"dale_chall\\\", \\\"ari\\\", \\\"flesch_reading_ease\\\"]\\n        \\n        for method in methods:\\n            # Extract scores for this method\\n            x_scores = np.array([d[\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan) for d in valid_clear])\\n            \\n            # Remove NaN values\\n            valid_idx = ~np.isnan(x_scores)\\n            x_valid = x_scores[valid_idx]\\n            y_valid = y_human[valid_idx]\\n            \\n            if len(x_valid) < 10:\\n                logger.warning(f\\\"  Insufficient valid data for {method}\\\")\\n                correlations[method] = {\\\"pearson_r\\\": np.nan, \\\"p_value\\\": np.nan, \\\"n\\\": 0}\\n                continue\\n            \\n            # Compute Pearson correlation\\n            r, p = pearsonr(x_valid, y_valid)\\n            \\n            # Bootstrap 95% CI for correlation\\n            def corr_func(data):\\n                return np.corrcoef(data[0], data[1])[0, 1]\\n            \\n            boot_result = bootstrap(\\n                data=(x_valid, y_valid),\\n                statistic=corr_func,\\n                confidence_level=0.95,\\n                n_resamples=1000,\\n                method='percentile'\\n            )\\n            \\n            correlations[method] = {\\n                \\\"pearson_r\\\": float(r),\\n                \\\"p_value\\\": float(p),\\n                \\\"ci_95_lower\\\": float(boot_result.confidence_interval.low),\\n                \\\"ci_95_upper\\\": float(boot_result.confidence_interval.high),\\n                \\\"n\\\": int(len(x_valid))\\n            }\\n            \\n            logger.info(f\\\"  {method}: r={r:.3f} (95% CI [{boot_result.confidence_interval.low:.3f}, {boot_result.confidence_interval.high:.3f}]), p={p:.4f}, n={len(x_valid)}\\\")\\n        \\n        evaluation_results[\\\"clear_corpus\\\"][\\\"correlations\\\"] = correlations\\n    \\n    # Extract valid examples (with difficulty levels)\\n    valid_ose = [d for d in ose_data if d[\\\"difficulty_level\\\"] is not None]\\n    logger.info(f\\\"  Valid examples for OneStopEnglish: {len(valid_ose)}/{len(ose_data)}\\\")\\n    \\n    if len(valid_ose) > 10:\\n        # Prepare data\\n        y_true = np.array([int(d[\\\"difficulty_level\\\"]) for d in valid_ose])  # 1, 2, or 3\\n        \\n        classification_results = {}\\n        \\n        for method in methods:\\n            # Extract scores\\n            x_scores = np.array([d[\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan) for d in valid_ose])\\n            \\n            # Remove NaN\\n            valid_idx = ~np.isnan(x_scores)\\n            x_valid = x_scores[valid_idx]\\n            y_valid = y_true[valid_idx]\\n            \\n            if len(x_valid) < 10:\\n                classification_results[method] = {\\\"accuracy\\\": np.nan, \\\"f1_macro\\\": np.nan, \\\"n\\\": 0}\\n                continue\\n            \\n            # Simple threshold-based classification\\n            # For readability scores: lower = easier (typically)\\n            # For SCD: higher = less coherent = harder (hypothesis)\\n            \\n            # Use median split for 3-class (simple baseline)\\n            if method.startswith(\\\"scd\\\"):\\n                # Higher SCD = harder, so invert for classification\\n                x_for_classify = -x_valid\\n            else:\\n                x_for_classify = x_valid\\n            \\n            # Simple classification: split into 3 quantiles\\n            from sklearn.tree import DecisionTreeClassifier\\n            from sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score\\n            \\n            clf = DecisionTreeClassifier(max_depth=3, random_state=42)\\n            cv_scores = cross_val_score(clf, x_for_classify.reshape(-1, 1), y_valid, cv=5, scoring='accuracy')\\n            cv_f1 = cross_val_score(clf, x_for_classify.reshape(-1, 1), y_valid, cv=5, scoring='f1_macro')\\n            \\n            classification_results[method] = {\\n                \\\"accuracy_mean\\\": float(np.mean(cv_scores)),\\n                \\\"accuracy_std\\\": float(np.std(cv_scores)),\\n                \\\"f1_macro_mean\\\": float(np.mean(cv_f1)),\\n                \\\"f1_macro_std\\\": float(np.std(cv_f1)),\\n                \\\"n\\\": int(len(x_valid))\\n            }\\n            \\n            logger.info(f\\\"  {method}: accuracy={np.mean(cv_scores):.3f} (+/- {np.std(cv_scores):.3f}), f1={np.mean(cv_f1):.3f}, n={len(x_valid)}\\\")\\n        \\n        evaluation_results[\\\"onestop_english\\\"][\\\"classification\\\"] = classification_results\\n    \\n    # Group by pair ID (wiki_simple_XXX and wiki_normal_XXX)\\n    pairs = {}\\n    for d in wiki_data:\\n        text_id = d[\\\"text_id\\\"]\\n        # Extract base ID\\n        if \\\"wiki_simple\\\" in text_id:\\n            base_id = text_id.replace(\\\"wiki_simple_\\\", \\\"\\\")\\n            pair_key = f\\\"pair_{base_id}\\\"\\n            if pair_key not in pairs:\\n                pairs[pair_key] = {}\\n            pairs[pair_key][\\\"simple\\\"] = d\\n        elif \\\"wiki_normal\\\" in text_id:\\n            base_id = text_id.replace(\\\"wiki_normal_\\\", \\\"\\\")\\n            pair_key = f\\\"pair_{base_id}\\\"\\n            if pair_key not in pairs:\\n                pairs[pair_key] = {}\\n            pairs[pair_key][\\\"normal\\\"] = d\\n    \\n    # Evaluate ranking (simple should have lower readability score than normal)\\n    ranking_results = {}\\n    \\n    for method in methods:\\n        correct = 0\\n        total = 0\\n        \\n        for pair_key, pair_data in pairs.items():\\n            if \\\"simple\\\" not in pair_data or \\\"normal\\\" not in pair_data:\\n                continue\\n            \\n            simple_score = pair_data[\\\"simple\\\"][\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan)\\n            normal_score = pair_data[\\\"normal\\\"][\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan)\\n            \\n            if np.isnan(simple_score) or np.isnan(normal_score):\\n                continue\\n            \\n            # For traditional formulas: simple < normal (lower grade level)\\n            # For SCD: hypothesis is that simple has lower SCD (more coherent)\\n            if method.startswith(\\\"scd\\\"):\\n                # Lower SCD = more coherent = simpler\\n                if simple_score < normal_score:\\n                    correct += 1\\n            else:\\n                # Lower grade level = simpler\\n                if simple_score < normal_score:\\n                    correct += 1\\n            \\n            total += 1\\n        \\n        if total > 0:\\n            accuracy = correct / total\\n        else:\\n            accuracy = np.nan\\n        \\n        ranking_results[method] = {\\n            \\\"ranking_accuracy\\\": float(accuracy),\\n            \\\"n_pairs\\\": int(total)\\n        }\\n        \\n        logger.info(f\\\"  {method}: ranking accuracy={accuracy:.3f} ({correct}/{total})\\\")\\n    \\n    evaluation_results[\\\"wikilarge\\\"][\\\"ranking\\\"] = ranking_results\\n    \\n    # Add trend line\\n            z = np.polyfit(x_valid, y_valid, 1)\\n            p_line = np.poly1d(z)\\n            x_range = np.linspace(x_valid.min(), x_valid.max(), 100)\\n            ax.plot(x_range, p_line(x_range), \\\"r--\\\", alpha=0.8)\\n        \\n        plt.tight_layout()\\n        plt.savefig(plots_dir / \\\"clear_corpus_scatter.png\\\", dpi=150)\\n        plt.close()\\n        \\n        logger.info(f\\\"  Saved scatter plot: {plots_dir / 'clear_corpus_scatter.png'}\\\")\\n    \\n    # Sentence tokenization using regex: `re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\\\\s+', text.strip())`\\\\n\\\\n2. SBERT encoding: `embeddings = model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)`\\\\n\\\\n3. Compute distances between consecutive sentences:\\\\n   - Cosine distance = 1 - cosine_similarity\\\\n   - Squared Euclidean distance = sum((emb[i+1] - emb[i])^2)\\\\n\\\\n4. =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 1: Load and Validate Data\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 1: Loading datasets...\\\")\\n    \\n    data_path = Path(\\\"../iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1/full_data_out.json\\\")\\n    with open(data_path, 'r') as f:\\n        data = json.load(f)\\n    \\n    # Extract datasets\\n    datasets = {d[\\\"dataset\\\"]: d[\\\"examples\\\"] for d in data[\\\"datasets\\\"]}\\n    \\n    logger.info(f\\\"Loaded datasets: {list(datasets.keys())}\\\")\\n    for name, examples in datasets.items():\\n        logger.info(f\\\"  {name}: {len(examples)} examples\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 2: Initialize Models\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 2: Initializing SBERT model...\\\")\\n    \\n    # Load SBERT model (all-MiniLM-L6-v2 = 384 dimensions, fast inference)\\n    sbert_model = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\\n    logger.info(f\\\"SBERT model loaded: {sbert_model.get_sentence_embedding_dimension()}D embeddings\\\")\\n    \\n    # Initialize textstat (no setup needed, but set language)\\n    textstat.set_lang('en')\\n    logger.info(\\\"textstat initialized\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 3: Implement SCD Metric\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 3: Implementing SCD computation...\\\")\\n    \\n    def sentence_tokenize(text: str) -> List[str]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Simple sentence tokenization.\\n        Splits on [.!?] followed by whitespace or end-of-string.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        # Split on sentence endings\\n        sentences = re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\\\\s+', text.strip())\\n        # Filter empty sentences\\n        sentences = [s.strip() for s in sentences if s.strip()]\\n        return sentences\\n    \\n    def compute_scd(text: str, method: str = \\\"cosine\\\") -> float:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute Semantic Coherence Distance for a text.\\n        \\n        Args:\\n            text: Input text\\n            method: \\\"cosine\\\" or \\\"euclidean\\\"\\n        \\n        Returns:\\n            SCD score (normalized by sentence count)\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        sentences = sentence_tokenize(text)\\n        \\n        if len(sentences) < 2:\\n            return 0.0  # Single sentence = perfect coherence\\n        \\n        # Encode sentences\\n        embeddings = sbert_model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n        \\n        # Compute pairwise distances between consecutive sentences\\n        distances = []\\n        for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n            if method == \\\"cosine\\\":\\n                # Cosine distance = 1 - cosine_similarity\\n                cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n                dist = 1 - cos_sim\\n            elif method == \\\"euclidean\\\":\\n                # Squared Euclidean distance\\n                diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n                dist = np.sum(diff**2)\\n            else:\\n                raise ValueError(f\\\"Unknown method: {method}\\\")\\n            distances.append(dist)\\n        \\n        # Average distance (normalize by sentence count)\\n        scd = np.mean(distances)\\n        return float(scd)\\n    \\n    def compute_scd_variants(text: str) -> Dict[str, float]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute multiple SCD variants for ablation.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        sentences = sentence_tokenize(text)\\n        if len(sentences) < 2:\\n            return {\\n                \\\"scd_cosine\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_euclidean\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_cosine_norm\\\": 0.0,\\n                \\\"scd_euclidean_norm\\\": 0.0,\\n            }\\n        \\n        embeddings = sbert_model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\\n        \\n        # Cosine distances\\n        cos_dists = []\\n        eucl_dists = []\\n        for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\\n            # Cosine\\n            cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\\n            cos_dists.append(1 - cos_sim)\\n            # Euclidean\\n            diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\\n            eucl_dists.append(np.sum(diff**2))\\n        \\n        return {\\n            \\\"scd_cosine\\\": np.mean(cos_dists),\\n            \\\"scd_euclidean\\\": np.mean(eucl_dists),\\n            \\\"scd_cosine_norm\\\": np.mean(cos_dists) / len(sentences),  # Normalize by sent count\\n            \\\"scd_euclidean_norm\\\": np.mean(eucl_dists) / len(sentences),\\n        }\\n    \\n    logger.info(\\\"SCD functions defined\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 4: Implement Baseline Readability Formulas\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 4: Implementing baseline readability formulas...\\\")\\n    \\n    def compute_readability_scores(text: str) -> Dict[str, float]:\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        Compute all baseline readability formulas using textstat.\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        scores = {}\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_kincaid\\\"] = textstat.flesch_kincaid_grade(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_kincaid\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"smog\\\"] = textstat.smog_index(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"smog\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"coleman_liau\\\"] = textstat.coleman_liau_index(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"coleman_liau\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"dale_chall\\\"] = textstat.dale_chall_readability_score(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"dale_chall\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"ari\\\"] = textstat.automated_readability_index(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"ari\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        try:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_reading_ease\\\"] = textstat.flesch_reading_ease(text)\\n        except:\\n            scores[\\\"flesch_reading_ease\\\"] = np.nan\\n        \\n        return scores\\n    \\n    logger.info(\\\"Baseline formulas defined\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 5: Compute Metrics for All Datasets\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 5: Computing metrics for all examples...\\\")\\n    \\n    results = {\\n        \\\"metadata\\\": {\\n            \\\"description\\\": \\\"SCD vs Baseline Readability Formulas Experiment\\\",\\n            \\\"datasets\\\": list(datasets.keys()),\\n            \\\"methods\\\": [\\\"scd_cosine\\\", \\\"scd_euclidean\\\", \\\"flesch_kincaid\\\", \\\"smog\\\", \\\"coleman_liau\\\", \\\"dale_chall\\\", \\\"ari\\\"]\\n        },\\n        \\\"results_by_dataset\\\": {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    for dataset_name, examples in datasets.items():\\n        logger.info(f\\\"Processing {dataset_name} ({len(examples)} examples)...\\\")\\n        \\n        dataset_results = []\\n        \\n        for i, example in enumerate(examples):\\n            if i % 100 == 0:\\n                logger.info(f\\\"  Processing example {i}/{len(examples)}...\\\")\\n            \\n            text = example[\\\"input\\\"]\\n            \\n            # Compute SCD variants\\n            scd_scores = compute_scd_variants(text)\\n            \\n            # Compute baseline readability scores\\n            readability_scores = compute_readability_scores(text)\\n            \\n            # Combine all scores\\n            all_scores = {**scd_scores, **readability_scores}\\n            \\n            # Store result\\n            result = {\\n                \\\"text_id\\\": example.get(\\\"metadata_text_id\\\", str(i)),\\n                \\\"text\\\": text[:200] + \\\"...\\\" if len(text) > 200 else text,  # Truncate for storage\\n                \\\"scores\\\": all_scores,\\n                \\\"human_readability\\\": float(example[\\\"output\\\"]) if example[\\\"output\\\"].replace('.', '').replace('-', '').isdigit() else None,\\n                \\\"difficulty_level\\\": example.get(\\\"metadata_difficulty\\\", None),\\n            }\\n            \\n            dataset_results.append(result)\\n        \\n        results[\\\"results_by_dataset\\\"][dataset_name] = dataset_results\\n        logger.info(f\\\"  Completed {dataset_name}\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 6: Statistical Evaluation\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 6: Computing correlations and classification metrics...\\\")\\n    \\n    evaluation_results = {\\n        \\\"clear_corpus\\\": {},\\n        \\\"onestop_english\\\": {},\\n        \\\"wikilarge\\\": {}\\n    }\\n    \\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    # CLEAR Corpus: Correlation with Human Judgments\\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    logger.info(\\\"Evaluating CLEAR Corpus (correlation with human judgments)...\\\")\\n    \\n    clear_data = results[\\\"results_by_dataset\\\"][\\\"clear_corpus\\\"]\\n    \\n    # Extract valid examples (with human readability scores)\\n    valid_clear = [d for d in clear_data if d[\\\"human_readability\\\"] is not None]\\n    logger.info(f\\\"  Valid examples for CLEAR: {len(valid_clear)}/{len(clear_data)}\\\")\\n    \\n    if len(valid_clear) > 10:\\n        # Prepare data for correlation\\n        y_human = np.array([d[\\\"human_readability\\\"] for d in valid_clear])\\n        \\n        correlations = {}\\n        \\n        # Methods to evaluate\\n        methods = [\\\"scd_cosine\\\", \\\"scd_euclidean\\\", \\\"flesch_kincaid\\\", \\\"smog\\\", \\\"coleman_liau\\\", \\\"dale_chall\\\", \\\"ari\\\", \\\"flesch_reading_ease\\\"]\\n        \\n        for method in methods:\\n            # Extract scores for this method\\n            x_scores = np.array([d[\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan) for d in valid_clear])\\n            \\n            # Remove NaN values\\n            valid_idx = ~np.isnan(x_scores)\\n            x_valid = x_scores[valid_idx]\\n            y_valid = y_human[valid_idx]\\n            \\n            if len(x_valid) < 10:\\n                logger.warning(f\\\"  Insufficient valid data for {method}\\\")\\n                correlations[method] = {\\\"pearson_r\\\": np.nan, \\\"p_value\\\": np.nan, \\\"n\\\": 0}\\n                continue\\n            \\n            # Compute Pearson correlation\\n            r, p = pearsonr(x_valid, y_valid)\\n            \\n            # Bootstrap 95% CI for correlation\\n            def corr_func(data):\\n                return np.corrcoef(data[0], data[1])[0, 1]\\n            \\n            boot_result = bootstrap(\\n                data=(x_valid, y_valid),\\n                statistic=corr_func,\\n                confidence_level=0.95,\\n                n_resamples=1000,\\n                method='percentile'\\n            )\\n            \\n            correlations[method] = {\\n                \\\"pearson_r\\\": float(r),\\n                \\\"p_value\\\": float(p),\\n                \\\"ci_95_lower\\\": float(boot_result.confidence_interval.low),\\n                \\\"ci_95_upper\\\": float(boot_result.confidence_interval.high),\\n                \\\"n\\\": int(len(x_valid))\\n            }\\n            \\n            logger.info(f\\\"  {method}: r={r:.3f} (95% CI [{boot_result.confidence_interval.low:.3f}, {boot_result.confidence_interval.high:.3f}]), p={p:.4f}, n={len(x_valid)}\\\")\\n        \\n        evaluation_results[\\\"clear_corpus\\\"][\\\"correlations\\\"] = correlations\\n    \\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    # OneStopEnglish: Classification (3 difficulty levels)\\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    logger.info(\\\"Evaluating OneStopEnglish (3-class classification)...\\\")\\n    \\n    ose_data = results[\\\"results_by_dataset\\\"][\\\"onestop_english\\\"]\\n    \\n    # Extract valid examples (with difficulty levels)\\n    valid_ose = [d for d in ose_data if d[\\\"difficulty_level\\\"] is not None]\\n    logger.info(f\\\"  Valid examples for OneStopEnglish: {len(valid_ose)}/{len(ose_data)}\\\")\\n    \\n    if len(valid_ose) > 10:\\n        # Prepare data\\n        y_true = np.array([int(d[\\\"difficulty_level\\\"]) for d in valid_ose])  # 1, 2, or 3\\n        \\n        classification_results = {}\\n        \\n        for method in methods:\\n            # Extract scores\\n            x_scores = np.array([d[\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan) for d in valid_ose])\\n            \\n            # Remove NaN\\n            valid_idx = ~np.isnan(x_scores)\\n            x_valid = x_scores[valid_idx]\\n            y_valid = y_true[valid_idx]\\n            \\n            if len(x_valid) < 10:\\n                classification_results[method] = {\\\"accuracy\\\": np.nan, \\\"f1_macro\\\": np.nan, \\\"n\\\": 0}\\n                continue\\n            \\n            # Simple threshold-based classification\\n            # For readability scores: lower = easier (typically)\\n            # For SCD: higher = less coherent = harder (hypothesis)\\n            \\n            # Use median split for 3-class (simple baseline)\\n            if method.startswith(\\\"scd\\\"):\\n                # Higher SCD = harder, so invert for classification\\n                x_for_classify = -x_valid\\n            else:\\n                x_for_classify = x_valid\\n            \\n            # Simple classification: split into 3 quantiles\\n            from sklearn.tree import DecisionTreeClassifier\\n            from sklearn.model_selection import cross_val_score\\n            \\n            clf = DecisionTreeClassifier(max_depth=3, random_state=42)\\n            cv_scores = cross_val_score(clf, x_for_classify.reshape(-1, 1), y_valid, cv=5, scoring='accuracy')\\n            cv_f1 = cross_val_score(clf, x_for_classify.reshape(-1, 1), y_valid, cv=5, scoring='f1_macro')\\n            \\n            classification_results[method] = {\\n                \\\"accuracy_mean\\\": float(np.mean(cv_scores)),\\n                \\\"accuracy_std\\\": float(np.std(cv_scores)),\\n                \\\"f1_macro_mean\\\": float(np.mean(cv_f1)),\\n                \\\"f1_macro_std\\\": float(np.std(cv_f1)),\\n                \\\"n\\\": int(len(x_valid))\\n            }\\n            \\n            logger.info(f\\\"  {method}: accuracy={np.mean(cv_scores):.3f} (+/- {np.std(cv_scores):.3f}), f1={np.mean(cv_f1):.3f}, n={len(x_valid)}\\\")\\n        \\n        evaluation_results[\\\"onestop_english\\\"][\\\"classification\\\"] = classification_results\\n    \\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    # WikiLarge: Simplification Pair Ranking\\n    # -------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n    logger.info(\\\"Evaluating WikiLarge (simplification pair ranking)...\\\")\\n    \\n    wiki_data = results[\\\"results_by_dataset\\\"][\\\"wikilarge\\\"]\\n    \\n    # Group by pair ID (wiki_simple_XXX and wiki_normal_XXX)\\n    pairs = {}\\n    for d in wiki_data:\\n        text_id = d[\\\"text_id\\\"]\\n        # Extract base ID\\n        if \\\"wiki_simple\\\" in text_id:\\n            base_id = text_id.replace(\\\"wiki_simple_\\\", \\\"\\\")\\n            pair_key = f\\\"pair_{base_id}\\\"\\n            if pair_key not in pairs:\\n                pairs[pair_key] = {}\\n            pairs[pair_key][\\\"simple\\\"] = d\\n        elif \\\"wiki_normal\\\" in text_id:\\n            base_id = text_id.replace(\\\"wiki_normal_\\\", \\\"\\\")\\n            pair_key = f\\\"pair_{base_id}\\\"\\n            if pair_key not in pairs:\\n                pairs[pair_key] = {}\\n            pairs[pair_key][\\\"normal\\\"] = d\\n    \\n    # Evaluate ranking (simple should have lower readability score than normal)\\n    ranking_results = {}\\n    \\n    for method in methods:\\n        correct = 0\\n        total = 0\\n        \\n        for pair_key, pair_data in pairs.items():\\n            if \\\"simple\\\" not in pair_data or \\\"normal\\\" not in pair_data:\\n                continue\\n            \\n            simple_score = pair_data[\\\"simple\\\"][\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan)\\n            normal_score = pair_data[\\\"normal\\\"][\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan)\\n            \\n            if np.isnan(simple_score) or np.isnan(normal_score):\\n                continue\\n            \\n            # For traditional formulas: simple < normal (lower grade level)\\n            # For SCD: hypothesis is that simple has lower SCD (more coherent)\\n            if method.startswith(\\\"scd\\\"):\\n                # Lower SCD = more coherent = simpler\\n                if simple_score < normal_score:\\n                    correct += 1\\n            else:\\n                # Lower grade level = simpler\\n                if simple_score < normal_score:\\n                    correct += 1\\n            \\n            total += 1\\n        \\n        if total > 0:\\n            accuracy = correct / total\\n        else:\\n            accuracy = np.nan\\n        \\n        ranking_results[method] = {\\n            \\\"ranking_accuracy\\\": float(accuracy),\\n            \\\"n_pairs\\\": int(total)\\n        }\\n        \\n        logger.info(f\\\"  {method}: ranking accuracy={accuracy:.3f} ({correct}/{total})\\\")\\n    \\n    evaluation_results[\\\"wikilarge\\\"][\\\"ranking\\\"] = ranking_results\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 7: Generate Visualizations\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 7: Generating scatter plots...\\\")\\n    \\n    # Create plots directory\\n    plots_dir = Path(\\\"plots\\\")\\n    plots_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\\n    \\n    # Plot 1: CLEAR Corpus - SCD vs Human Judgments\\n    if len(valid_clear) > 10:\\n        fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 2, figsize=(12, 10))\\n        fig.suptitle(\\\"CLEAR Corpus: SCD and Baselines vs Human Readability\\\", fontsize=14)\\n        \\n        plot_methods = [\\\"scd_cosine\\\", \\\"scd_euclidean\\\", \\\"flesch_kincaid\\\", \\\"smog\\\"]\\n        \\n        for idx, method in enumerate(plot_methods):\\n            ax = axes[idx // 2, idx % 2]\\n            \\n            x_scores = np.array([d[\\\"scores\\\"].get(method, np.nan) for d in valid_clear])\\n            valid_idx = ~np.isnan(x_scores)\\n            x_valid = x_scores[valid_idx]\\n            y_valid = y_human[valid_idx]\\n            \\n            ax.scatter(x_valid, y_valid, alpha=0.5, s=10)\\n            ax.set_xlabel(method)\\n            ax.set_ylabel(\\\"Human Readability Score\\\")\\n            \\n            # Add correlation coefficient to plot\\n            r = correlations[method][\\\"pearson_r\\\"]\\n            p = correlations[method][\\\"p_value\\\"]\\n            ax.set_title(f\\\"{method}: r={r:.3f} (p={p:.4f})\\\")\\n            \\n            # Add trend line\\n            z = np.polyfit(x_valid, y_valid, 1)\\n            p_line = np.poly1d(z)\\n            x_range = np.linspace(x_valid.min(), x_valid.max(), 100)\\n            ax.plot(x_range, p_line(x_range), \\\"r--\\\", alpha=0.8)\\n        \\n        plt.tight_layout()\\n        plt.savefig(plots_dir / \\\"clear_corpus_scatter.png\\\", dpi=150)\\n        plt.close()\\n        \\n        logger.info(f\\\"  Saved scatter plot: {plots_dir / 'clear_corpus_scatter.png'}\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 8: Timing Benchmark\\n    # =========================================================================\\n    logger.info(\\\"Phase 8: Timing benchmark...\\\")\\n    \\n    timing_results = {}\\n    \\n    # Time SCD computation\\n    test_text = valid_clear[0][\\\"text\\\"] if valid_clear else \\\"This is a test sentence. This is another sentence.\\\"\\n    \\n    # Time SBERT encoding\\n    start = time.time()\\n    for _ in range(10):\\n        _ = sbert_model.encode(sentence_tokenize(test_text), show_progress_bar=False)\\n    sbert_time = (time.time() - start) / 10\\n    \\n    # Time textstat\\n    start = time.time()\\n    for _ in range(10):\\n        _ = compute_readability_scores(test_text)\\n    textstat_time = (time.time() - start) / 10\\n    \\n    timing_results = {\\n        \\\"sbert_encoding_per_doc\\\": float(sbert_time),\\n        \\\"textstat_per_doc\\\": float(textstat_time),\\n        \\\"notes\\\": \\\"Average over 10 runs on sample document\\\"\\n    }\\n    \\n    logger.info(f\\\"  SBERT encoding: {sbert_time*1000:.1f}ms per doc\\\")\\n    logger.info(f\\\"  textstat: {textstat_time*1000:.1f}ms per doc\\\")\\n    \\n    # =========================================================================\\n    # PHASE 9: Save Sentence tokenization using regex: `re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\\\\s+', text.strip())`\\\\n\\\\n2. SBERT encoding: `embeddings = model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)`\\\\n\\\\n3. Compute distances between consecutive sentences:\\\\n   - Cosine distance = 1 - cosine_similarity\\\\n   - Squared Euclidean distance = sum((emb[i+1] - emb[i])^2)\\\\n\\\\n4. Load the standardized dataset from the dependency artifact:\n   - Path: `../iter_1/gen_art/gen_art_dataset_1/full_data_out.json`\n   - Use `Path()` from pathlib for cross-platform compatibility\n   - Parse JSON and extract the three datasets: clear_corpus, onestop_english, wikilarge\n\n2. Validate data structure:\n   - Check that each dataset has 'input' (text) and 'output' (readability score) fields\n   - For CLEAR: output is a float (human readability judgment)\n   - For OneStopEnglish: output is 1, 2, or 3 (difficulty level)\n   - For WikiLarge: output is 2 or 4 (difficulty level)\n\n## Phase 2: Model Initialization\n\n1. Initialize SBERT model:\n   ```python\n   from sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer\n   model = SentenceTransformer('all-MiniLM-L6-v2')\n   ```\n   - Model dimensions: 384\n   - Fast inference speed\n   - Cache location: ~/.cache/huggingface/transformers/\n\n2. Initialize textstat:\n   ```python\n   import textstat\n   textstat.set_lang('en')\n   ```\n   - No download required\n   - Works offline\n\n## Phase 3: SCD Metric Implementation\n\nImplement the `compute_scd_variants(text)` function:\n\n1. Sentence tokenization:\n   ```python\n   import re\n   sentences = re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\\\\s+', text.strip())\n   sentences = [s.strip() for s in sentences if s.strip()]\n   ```\n   - Handles '.', '!', '?' as sentence terminators\n   - Filters empty strings\n\n2. SBERT encoding:\n   ```python\n   embeddings = model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\n   ```\n   - Returns numpy array of shape (n_sentences, 384)\n   - Batch processing is automatic\n\n3. Compute distances between consecutive sentences:\n   ```python\n   cos_dists = []\n   eucl_dists = []\n   for i in range(len(embeddings) - 1):\n       # Cosine distance = 1 - cosine_similarity\n       cos_sim = np.dot(embeddings[i], embeddings[i+1]) / (np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i]) * np.linalg.norm(embeddings[i+1]))\n       cos_dists.append(1 - cos_sim)\n       \n       # Squared Euclidean distance\n       diff = embeddings[i+1] - embeddings[i]\n       eucl_dists.append(np.sum(diff**2))\n   ```\n\n4. Return variants:\n   ```python\n   return {\n       'scd_cosine': np.mean(cos_dists),\n       'scd_euclidean': np.mean(eucl_dists),\n       'scd_cosine_norm': np.mean(cos_dists) / len(sentences),\n       'scd_euclidean_norm': np.mean(eucl_dists) / len(sentences),\n   }\n   ```\n\n## Phase 4: Baseline Readability Formulas\n\nImplement `compute_readability_scores(text)` function using textstat:\n\n```python\ndef compute_readability_scores(text):\n    scores = {}\n    try:\n        scores['flesch_kincaid'] = textstat.flesch_kincaid_grade(text)\n    except:\n        scores['flesch_kincaid'] = np.nan\n    # Repeat for: smog, coleman_liau, dale_chall, ari, flesch_reading_ease\n    return scores\n```\n\nFormulas implemented:\n1. Flesch-Kincaid Grade Level\n2. SMOG Index\n3. Coleman-Liau Index\n4. Dale-Chall Readability Score\n5. Automated Readability Index\n6. Flesch Reading Ease\n\nUse try/except to handle errors (empty text, single words, etc.)\n\n## Phase 5: Compute Metrics for All Datasets\n\nFor each dataset and each example:\n1. Call `compute_scd_variants(text)` to get SCD scores\n2. Call `compute_readability_scores(text)` to get baseline scores\n3. Store results with metadata\n\nOutput structure:\n```python\nresults = {\n    'metadata': {...},\n    'results_by_dataset': {\n        'clear_corpus': [...],\n        'onestop_english': [...],\n        'wikilarge': [...]\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Phase 6: Statistical Evaluation\n\n### 6.1 CLEAR Corpus: Correlation with Human Judgments\n\n1. Extract valid examples (where `human_readability` is not None)\n2. For each method (scd_cosine, scd_euclidean, flesch_kincaid, etc.):\n   - Extract scores and human judgments\n   - Remove NaN values\n   - Compute Pearson correlation using `scipy.stats.pearsonr()`\n   - Compute 95% bootstrap confidence interval:\n     ```python\n     from scipy.stats import bootstrap\n     boot_result = bootstrap(\n         data=(x_scores, y_human),\n         statistic=lambda data: np.corrcoef(data[0], data[1])[0, 1],\n         confidence_level=0.95,\n         n_resamples=1000\n     )\n     ```\n   - Store: pearson_r, p_value, ci_95_lower, ci_95_upper, n\n\n### 6.2 OneStopEnglish: 3-Class Classification\n\n1. Extract valid examples (where `difficulty_level` is not None)\n2. For each method:\n   - Extract scores and difficulty levels (1, 2, 3)\n   - For SCD methods: invert scores (higher SCD = harder)\n   - Use DecisionTreeClassifier with 5-fold cross-validation\n   - Compute: accuracy (mean, std), f1_macro (mean, std)\n\n### 6.3 WikiLarge: Simplification Pair Ranking\n\n1. Group examples by pair ID (wiki_simple_XXX and wiki_normal_XXX)\n2. For each method:\n   - Compare scores for simple vs normal version\n   - For traditional formulas: simple should have LOWER score\n   - For SCD: simple should have LOWER score (hypothesis)\n   - Compute ranking accuracy (percentage of pairs correctly ranked)\n\n## Phase 7: Generate Visualizations\n\n1. Create `plots/` directory\n2. Generate scatter plots for CLEAR corpus:\n   ```python\n   fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 2, figsize=(12, 10))\n   # Plot scd_cosine, scd_euclidean, flesch_kincaid, smog\n   for idx, method in enumerate(plot_methods):\n       ax.scatter(x_scores, y_human, alpha=0.5, s=10)\n       ax.set_xlabel(method)\n       ax.set_ylabel('Human Readability Score')\n       ax.set_title(f'{method}: r={r:.3f} (p={p:.4f})')\n       # Add trend line\n       z = np.polyfit(x_valid, y_valid, 1)\n       ax.plot(x_range, np.poly1d(z)(x_range), 'r--', alpha=0.8)\n   plt.tight_layout()\n   plt.savefig('plots/clear_corpus_scatter.png', dpi=150)\n   ```\n\n## Phase 8: Timing Benchmark\n\n1. Time SBERT encoding:\n   ```python\n   start = time.time()\n   for _ in range(10):\n       model.encode(sentences, show_progress_bar=False)\n   sbert_time = (time.time() - start) / 10\n   ```\n\n2. Time textstat computation:\n   ```python\n   start = time.time()\n   for _ in range(10):\n       compute_readability_scores(test_text)\n   textstat_time = (time.time() - start) / 10\n   ```\n\n3. Log results in milliseconds per document\n\n## Phase 9: Save Results\n\n1.
